ADWeakPlaneStress

under construction:Undocumented Class

The ADWeakPlaneStress has not been documented. The content listed below should be used as a starting point for documenting the class, which includes the typical automatic documentation associated with a MooseObject; however, what is contained is ultimately determined by what is necessary to make the documentation clear for users.


# ADWeakPlaneStress

!syntax description /Kernels/ADWeakPlaneStress

## Overview

!! Replace these lines with information regarding the ADWeakPlaneStress object.

## Example Input File Syntax

!! Describe and include an example of how to use the ADWeakPlaneStress object.

!syntax parameters /Kernels/ADWeakPlaneStress

!syntax inputs /Kernels/ADWeakPlaneStress

!syntax children /Kernels/ADWeakPlaneStress

Plane stress kernel to provide out-of-plane strain contribution

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_exp_cartesian_5_5_rho_0_sample_10.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_5_5_rho_0_sample_10.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'

  [../]

  [../]

    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]

  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'boundary'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'boundary'
  [../]

  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]

    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'

      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

  [../]

[Kernels]

    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]

    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D_sensitivity/Gc_constant_rho_0.5/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = '../gold/Gc_sqexp_Gc_constant_rho_0.5_sample_1.txt'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = '../gold/psic_sqexp_Gc_constant_rho_0.5_sample_1.txt'
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = 'Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./length_scale]
    type = GenericConstantMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length'
    prop_values = '0.5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]

    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]

    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]

  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D/sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_4/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_4.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_4.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]

    d = 'd'

  [../]

  [../]

  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200        200                0                     vinewtonrsls'
  dt = 1e-3
  end_time = 0.22

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-12
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-08

  fp_max_its = 10
  fp_tol = 1e-03

  automatic_scaling = true
  compute_scaling_once = false
[]

[Outputs]
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    file_base = 'visualize'
    hide = 'bounds_dummy'
  [../]
  [./console]
    type = Console
    outlier_variable_norms = false
  [../]

    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]

    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]

    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation

    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]

  [../]

    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]

      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]

      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]

      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]

    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress

    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]

    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit

    d = d

    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_exp_cartesian_5_5_rho_0.5_sample_8.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_5_5_rho_0.5_sample_8.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    d = d
  [../]

    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

  [../]

    variable = 'E_el'

  [../]

    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]

    d = d
  [../]

      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [../]
[]

  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]

examples/mud_2D/exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_9/mechanical.i

[Functions]
  [./Gc]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/Gc_exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_9.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_9.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  print_linear_residuals = false

    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]

    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = '0.5 Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = StationaryGenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'phase_field_regularization_length energy_release_rate b'
    prop_values = '0.5 Gc psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]

    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

  [../]

    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]

    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]

    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]

      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]

  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

examples/mud_2D/sqexp_cartesian_20_20_rho_0_sample_3/mechanical.i

examples/traction_free/mechanical.i

[GlobalParams]
  displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = 'gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    # d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
    output_properties = stress
    outputs = exodus
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = '3e-5'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 8e-4
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  # petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  exodus = true
  print_linear_residuals = false
[]
Close

    data_file = ../gold/Gc_exp_cartesian_10_10_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = PiecewiseMultilinear
    data_file = ../gold/psic_exp_cartesian_10_10_rho_0_sample_6.txt
  [../]
[]

[Mesh]
  type = FileMesh
  file = '../gold/geo.msh'
[]

[Variables]
  [./disp_x]
  [../]
  [./disp_y]
  [../]
  [./strain_zz]
  [../]
[]

[AuxVariables]
  [./d]
  [../]
  [./load]
    family = SCALAR
  [../]
  [./E_el]
    order = CONSTANT
    family = MONOMIAL
  [../]
  [./Gc]
  [../]
  [./psic]
  [../]
[]

[AuxKernels]
  [./E_el]
    type = MaterialRealAux
    property = 'E_el'
    variable = 'E_el'
    execute_on = 'TIMESTEP_END'
  [../]
  [./Gc]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = Gc
    function = Gc
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
  [./psic]
    type = FunctionAux
    variable = psic
    function = psic
    execute_on = 'INITIAL'
  [../]
[]

[Kernels]
  [./solid_x]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_x
    component = 0
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./solid_y]
    type = ADStressDivergenceTensors
    variable = disp_y
    component = 1
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./plane_stress]
    type = ADWeakPlaneStress
    variable = strain_zz
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./react_x]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_x
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
  [./react_y]
    type = DegradedCoefReaction
    variable = disp_y
    coefficient = 0.1
  [../]
[]

[BCs]
  [./Periodic]
    [./x_left_right]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./y_left_right]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'left'
      secondary = 'right'
      translation = '100 0 0'
    [../]
    [./x_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_x
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
    [./y_top_bottom]
      variable = disp_y
      primary = 'top'
      secondary = 'bottom'
      translation = '0 -100 0'
    [../]
  [../]
  [./x_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_x
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center'
  [../]
  [./y_pin]
    type = DirichletBC
    variable = disp_y
    value = 0
    boundary = 'center pin'
  [../]
[]

[Materials]
  [./eigen_strain]
    type = ComputeEigenstrainFromScalarInitialStress
    initial_stress_xx = load
    initial_stress_yy = load
    eigenstrain_name = is
  [../]
  [./elasticity_tensor]
    type = ComputeIsotropicElasticityTensor
    poissons_ratio = 0.2
    youngs_modulus = 4
  [../]
  [./strain]
    type = ADComputePlaneSmallStrain
    out_of_plane_strain = strain_zz
    eigenstrain_names = is
    displacements = 'disp_x disp_y'
  [../]
  [./stress]
    type = SmallStrainDegradedPK2Stress_NoSplit
    d = d
    d_crit = 0.6
    history = false
  [../]
  [./fracture_energy_barrier]
    type = GenericFunctionMaterial
    prop_names = 'b'
    prop_values = 'psic'
  [../]
  [./local_dissipation]
    type = LinearLocalDissipation
    d = d
  [../]
  [./fracture_properties]
    type = FractureMaterial
    Gc = 'Gc'
    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]
  [./degradation]
    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

[Executioner]
  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'
  # petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type'
  # petsc_options_value = 'lu'
  petsc_options_iname = '-pc_type -sub_pc_type -ksp_max_it -ksp_gmres_restart -sub_pc_factor_levels'
  petsc_options_value = 'asm      ilu          200         200                0                    '
  dt = 1e-4

  nl_abs_tol = 1e-10
  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06

  automatic_scaling = true
[]

[Outputs]
  hide = 'load'
  print_linear_residuals = false
  [./exodus]
    type = Exodus
    execute_on = 'FINAL'
  [../]
[]
Close

    prop_names = 'b'

    d = d
  [../]

    L = 0.5
    local_dissipation_norm = 8/3
  [../]

    type = LorentzDegradation
    d = d
    residual_degradation = 1e-06
  [../]
[]

  type = Transient
  solve_type = 'NEWTON'

  nl_rel_tol = 1e-06
